{"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01K8ieDukaHCXJbbgRnX3V5b","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→//! Generation number management for read/compact race safety.\n     2→//!\n     3→//! Prevents race conditions where a reader opens the WAL file and a compactor\n     4→//! truncates it mid-read. Generation numbers ensure readers see consistent state:\n     5→//!\n     6→//! 1. Each compaction increments the generation number\n     7→//! 2. Readers check generation before and after reading\n     8→//! 3. If generation changed during read, retry with new generation\n     9→//!\n    10→//! File layout:\n    11→//!   .beads/beads.generation  - Contains current generation number (u64)\n    12→//!   .beads/beads.wal.N       - WAL file for generation N\n    13→\n    14→const std = @import(\"std\");\n    15→const fs = std.fs;\n    16→const BeadsLock = @import(\"lock.zig\").BeadsLock;\n    17→const test_util = @import(\"../test_util.zig\");\n    18→\n    19→pub const GenerationError = error{\n    20→    ReadFailed,\n    21→    WriteFailed,\n    22→    InvalidFormat,\n    23→    LockFailed,\n    24→    OutOfMemory,\n    25→};\n    26→\n    27→/// Manages generation numbers for WAL file rotation.\n    28→pub const Generation = struct {\n    29→    beads_dir: []const u8,\n    30→    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    31→\n    32→    const Self = @This();\n    33→\n    34→    /// File name for the generation number file.\n    35→    const GENERATION_FILE = \"beads.generation\";\n    36→\n    37→    /// Minimum generation number (starts at 1, never 0).\n    38→    const MIN_GENERATION: u64 = 1;\n    39→\n    40→    pub fn init(beads_dir: []const u8, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) Self {\n    41→        return .{\n    42→            .beads_dir = beads_dir,\n    43→            .allocator = allocator,\n    44→        };\n    45→    }\n    46→\n    47→    /// Read the current generation number.\n    48→    /// Returns MIN_GENERATION if file doesn't exist (fresh install).\n    49→    pub fn read(self: *Self) GenerationError!u64 {\n    50→        const gen_path = std.fs.path.join(self.allocator, &.{ self.beads_dir, GENERATION_FILE }) catch return GenerationError.OutOfMemory;\n    51→        defer self.allocator.free(gen_path);\n    52→\n    53→        const file = fs.cwd().openFile(gen_path, .{}) catch |err| switch (err) {\n    54→            error.FileNotFound => return MIN_GENERATION,\n    55→            else => return GenerationError.ReadFailed,\n    56→        };\n    57→        defer file.close();\n    58→\n    59→        var buf: [32]u8 = undefined;\n    60→        const bytes_read = file.readAll(&buf) catch return GenerationError.ReadFailed;\n    61→        if (bytes_read == 0) return MIN_GENERATION;\n    62→\n    63→        // Trim whitespace/newlines\n    64→        const content = std.mem.trim(u8, buf[0..bytes_read], \" \\t\\n\\r\");\n    65→        if (content.len == 0) return MIN_GENERATION;\n    66→\n    67→        return std.fmt.parseInt(u64, content, 10) catch return GenerationError.InvalidFormat;\n    68→    }\n    69→\n    70→    /// Write the generation number atomically.\n    71→    /// Uses temp file + rename pattern for crash safety.\n    72→    pub fn write(self: *Self, generation: u64) GenerationError!void {\n    73→        const gen_path = std.fs.path.join(self.allocator, &.{ self.beads_dir, GENERATION_FILE }) catch return GenerationError.OutOfMemory;\n    74→        defer self.allocator.free(gen_path);\n    75→\n    76→        const dir = fs.cwd();\n    77→\n    78→        // Ensure parent directory exists\n    79→        dir.makePath(self.beads_dir) catch |err| switch (err) {\n    80→            error.PathAlreadyExists => {},\n    81→            else => return GenerationError.WriteFailed,\n    82→        };\n    83→\n    84→        // Write to temp file first\n    85→        var tmp_path_buf: [std.fs.max_path_bytes]u8 = undefined;\n    86→        const tmp_path = std.fmt.bufPrint(&tmp_path_buf, \"{s}.tmp.{d}\", .{\n    87→            gen_path,\n    88→            std.time.milliTimestamp(),\n    89→        }) catch return GenerationError.WriteFailed;\n    90→\n    91→        const tmp_file = dir.createFile(tmp_path, .{}) catch return GenerationError.WriteFailed;\n    92→        errdefer {\n    93→            tmp_file.close();\n    94→            dir.deleteFile(tmp_path) catch {};\n    95→        }\n    96→\n    97→        // Write generation number\n    98→        var num_buf: [20]u8 = undefined;\n    99→        const num_str = std.fmt.bufPrint(&num_buf, \"{d}\\n\", .{generation}) catch return GenerationError.WriteFailed;\n   100→        tmp_file.writeAll(num_str) catch return GenerationError.WriteFailed;\n   101→\n   102→        // fsync for durability\n   103→        tmp_file.sync() catch return GenerationError.WriteFailed;\n   104→        tmp_file.close();\n   105→\n   106→        // Atomic rename\n   107→        dir.rename(tmp_path, gen_path) catch return GenerationError.WriteFailed;\n   108→    }\n   109→\n   110→    /// Increment generation atomically (under lock).\n   111→    /// Returns the new generation number.\n   112→    /// WARNING: This acquires a lock - do not call if you already hold the lock.\n   113→    pub fn increment(self: *Self, lock_path: []const u8) GenerationError!u64 {\n   114→        var lock = BeadsLock.acquire(lock_path) catch return GenerationError.LockFailed;\n   115→        defer lock.release();\n   116→\n   117→        return self.incrementUnlocked();\n   118→    }\n   119→\n   120→    /// Increment generation without acquiring a lock.\n   121→    /// Caller must already hold the exclusive lock.\n   122→    pub fn incrementUnlocked(self: *Self) GenerationError!u64 {\n   123→        const current = try self.read();\n   124→        const next = current + 1;\n   125→        try self.write(next);\n   126→        return next;\n   127→    }\n   128→\n   129→    /// Get the WAL file path for a specific generation.\n   130→    pub fn walPath(self: *Self, generation: u64) ![]const u8 {\n   131→        return std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, \"{s}/beads.wal.{d}\", .{ self.beads_dir, generation });\n   132→    }\n   133→\n   134→    /// Get the WAL file path for the current generation.\n   135→    pub fn currentWalPath(self: *Self) ![]const u8 {\n   136→        const gen = try self.read();\n   137→        return self.walPath(gen);\n   138→    }\n   139→\n   140→    /// Clean up old WAL files (keep only current and previous generation).\n   141→    /// Should be called after successful compaction.\n   142→    pub fn cleanupOldGenerations(self: *Self, current_gen: u64) void {\n   143→        if (current_gen <= 2) return; // Nothing to clean up\n   144→\n   145→        // Delete WAL files older than current - 1\n   146→        const cleanup_gen = current_gen - 2;\n   147→        const wal_path = self.walPath(cleanup_gen) catch return;\n   148→        defer self.allocator.free(wal_path);\n   149→\n   150→        fs.cwd().deleteFile(wal_path) catch {};\n   151→    }\n   152→};\n   153→\n   154→/// Load state with generation-based consistency checking.\n   155→/// Retries if generation changes during read (compaction happened mid-read).\n   156→pub const GenerationAwareLoader = struct {\n   157→    beads_dir: []const u8,\n   158→    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n   159→    max_retries: u32 = 3,\n   160→\n   161→    const Self = @This();\n   162→\n   163→    pub fn init(beads_dir: []const u8, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) Self {\n   164→        return .{\n   165→            .beads_dir = beads_dir,\n   166→            .allocator = allocator,\n   167→        };\n   168→    }\n   169→\n   170→    /// Result of a generation-aware load operation.\n   171→    pub const LoadResult = struct {\n   172→        generation: u64,\n   173→        wal_path: []const u8,\n   174→        retried: bool,\n   175→\n   176→        pub fn deinit(self: *LoadResult, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) void {\n   177→            allocator.free(self.wal_path);\n   178→        }\n   179→    };\n   180→\n   181→    /// Get current generation and WAL path with retry on generation change.\n   182→    /// Returns the generation that was successfully read without concurrent change.\n   183→    pub fn getConsistentGeneration(self: *Self) !LoadResult {\n   184→        var gen = Generation.init(self.beads_dir, self.allocator);\n   185→        var retried = false;\n   186→\n   187→        var attempts: u32 = 0;\n   188→        while (attempts < self.max_retries) : (attempts += 1) {\n   189→            // Read generation before loading\n   190→            const gen_before = try gen.read();\n   191→            const wal_path = try gen.walPath(gen_before);\n   192→            errdefer self.allocator.free(wal_path);\n   193→\n   194→            // Read generation after loading\n   195→            const gen_after = try gen.read();\n   196→\n   197→            if (gen_before == gen_after) {\n   198→                // Generation stable - return consistent state\n   199→                return LoadResult{\n   200→                    .generation = gen_before,\n   201→                    .wal_path = wal_path,\n   202→                    .retried = retried,\n   203→                };\n   204→            }\n   205→\n   206→            // Generation changed during read - retry\n   207→            self.allocator.free(wal_path);\n   208→            retried = true;\n   209→        }\n   210→\n   211→        // Max retries exceeded - return latest generation\n   212→        // (this should be very rare, only under extreme compaction load)\n   213→        const final_gen = try gen.read();\n   214→        return LoadResult{\n   215→            .generation = final_gen,\n   216→            .wal_path = try gen.walPath(final_gen),\n   217→            .retried = retried,\n   218→        };\n   219→    }\n   220→};\n   221→\n   222→// --- Tests ---\n   223→\n   224→test \"Generation.read returns MIN_GENERATION for missing file\" {\n   225→    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n   226→    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"gen_missing\");\n   227→    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n   228→    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n   229→\n   230→    var gen = Generation.init(test_dir, allocator);\n   231→    const value = try gen.read();\n   232→    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u64, 1), Generation number management for read/compact race safety.\n//!\n//! Prevents race conditions where a reader opens the WAL file and a compactor\n//! truncates it mid-read. Generation numbers ensure readers see consistent state:\n//!\n//! 1. Each compaction increments the generation number\n//! 2. Readers check generation before and after reading\n//! 3. If generation changed during read, retry with new generation\n//!\n//! File layout:\n//!   .beads/beads.generation  - Contains current generation number (u64)\n//!   .beads/beads.wal.N       - WAL file for generation N\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\nconst fs = std.fs;\nconst BeadsLock = @import(\"lock.zig\").BeadsLock;\nconst test_util = @import(\"../test_util.zig\");\n\npub const GenerationError = error{\n    ReadFailed,\n    WriteFailed,\n    InvalidFormat,\n    LockFailed,\n    OutOfMemory,\n};\n\n/// Manages generation numbers for WAL file rotation.\npub const Generation = struct {\n    beads_dir: []const u8,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n\n    const Self = @This();\n\n    /// File name for the generation number file.\n    const GENERATION_FILE = \"beads.generation\";\n\n    /// Minimum generation number (starts at 1, never 0).\n    const MIN_GENERATION: u64 = 1;\n\n    pub fn init(beads_dir: []const u8, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) Self {\n        return .{\n            .beads_dir = beads_dir,\n            .allocator = allocator,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Read the current generation number.\n    /// Returns MIN_GENERATION if file doesn't exist (fresh install).\n    pub fn read(self: *Self) GenerationError!u64 {\n        const gen_path = std.fs.path.join(self.allocator, &.{ self.beads_dir, GENERATION_FILE }) catch return GenerationError.OutOfMemory;\n        defer self.allocator.free(gen_path);\n\n        const file = fs.cwd().openFile(gen_path, .{}) catch |err| switch (err) {\n            error.FileNotFound => return MIN_GENERATION,\n            else => return GenerationError.ReadFailed,\n        };\n        defer file.close();\n\n        var buf: [32]u8 = undefined;\n        const bytes_read = file.readAll(&buf) catch return GenerationError.ReadFailed;\n        if (bytes_read == 0) return MIN_GENERATION;\n\n        // Trim whitespace/newlines\n        const content = std.mem.trim(u8, buf[0..bytes_read], \" \\t\\n\\r\");\n        if (content.len == 0) return MIN_GENERATION;\n\n        return std.fmt.parseInt(u64, content, 10) catch return GenerationError.InvalidFormat;\n    }\n\n    /// Write the generation number atomically.\n    /// Uses temp file + rename pattern for crash safety.\n    pub fn write(self: *Self, generation: u64) GenerationError!void {\n        const gen_path = std.fs.path.join(self.allocator, &.{ self.beads_dir, GENERATION_FILE }) catch return GenerationError.OutOfMemory;\n        defer self.allocator.free(gen_path);\n\n        const dir = fs.cwd();\n\n        // Ensure parent directory exists\n        dir.makePath(self.beads_dir) catch |err| switch (err) {\n            error.PathAlreadyExists => {},\n            else => return GenerationError.WriteFailed,\n        };\n\n        // Write to temp file first\n        var tmp_path_buf: [std.fs.max_path_bytes]u8 = undefined;\n        const tmp_path = std.fmt.bufPrint(&tmp_path_buf, \"{s}.tmp.{d}\", .{\n            gen_path,\n            std.time.milliTimestamp(),\n        }) catch return GenerationError.WriteFailed;\n\n        const tmp_file = dir.createFile(tmp_path, .{}) catch return GenerationError.WriteFailed;\n        errdefer {\n            tmp_file.close();\n            dir.deleteFile(tmp_path) catch {};\n        }\n\n        // Write generation number\n        var num_buf: [20]u8 = undefined;\n        const num_str = std.fmt.bufPrint(&num_buf, \"{d}\\n\", .{generation}) catch return GenerationError.WriteFailed;\n        tmp_file.writeAll(num_str) catch return GenerationError.WriteFailed;\n\n        // fsync for durability\n        tmp_file.sync() catch return GenerationError.WriteFailed;\n        tmp_file.close();\n\n        // Atomic rename\n        dir.rename(tmp_path, gen_path) catch return GenerationError.WriteFailed;\n    }\n\n    /// Increment generation atomically (under lock).\n    /// Returns the new generation number.\n    /// WARNING: This acquires a lock - do not call if you already hold the lock.\n    pub fn increment(self: *Self, lock_path: []const u8) GenerationError!u64 {\n        var lock = BeadsLock.acquire(lock_path) catch return GenerationError.LockFailed;\n        defer lock.release();\n\n        return self.incrementUnlocked();\n    }\n\n    /// Increment generation without acquiring a lock.\n    /// Caller must already hold the exclusive lock.\n    pub fn incrementUnlocked(self: *Self) GenerationError!u64 {\n        const current = try self.read();\n        const next = current + 1;\n        try self.write(next);\n        return next;\n    }\n\n    /// Get the WAL file path for a specific generation.\n    pub fn walPath(self: *Self, generation: u64) ![]const u8 {\n        return std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, \"{s}/beads.wal.{d}\", .{ self.beads_dir, generation });\n    }\n\n    /// Get the WAL file path for the current generation.\n    pub fn currentWalPath(self: *Self) ![]const u8 {\n        const gen = try self.read();\n        return self.walPath(gen);\n    }\n\n    /// Clean up old WAL files (keep only current and previous generation).\n    /// Should be called after successful compaction.\n    pub fn cleanupOldGenerations(self: *Self, current_gen: u64) void {\n        if (current_gen <= 2) return; // Nothing to clean up\n\n        // Delete WAL files older than current - 1\n        const cleanup_gen = current_gen - 2;\n        const wal_path = self.walPath(cleanup_gen) catch return;\n        defer self.allocator.free(wal_path);\n\n        fs.cwd().deleteFile(wal_path) catch {};\n    }\n};\n\n/// Load state with generation-based consistency checking.\n/// Retries if generation changes during read (compaction happened mid-read).\npub const GenerationAwareLoader = struct {\n    beads_dir: []const u8,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    max_retries: u32 = 3,\n\n    const Self = @This();\n\n    pub fn init(beads_dir: []const u8, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) Self {\n        return .{\n            .beads_dir = beads_dir,\n            .allocator = allocator,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Result of a generation-aware load operation.\n    pub const LoadResult = struct {\n        generation: u64,\n        wal_path: []const u8,\n        retried: bool,\n\n        pub fn deinit(self: *LoadResult, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) void {\n            allocator.free(self.wal_path);\n        }\n    };\n\n    /// Get current generation and WAL path with retry on generation change.\n    /// Returns the generation that was successfully read without concurrent change.\n    pub fn getConsistentGeneration(self: *Self) !LoadResult {\n        var gen = Generation.init(self.beads_dir, self.allocator);\n        var retried = false;\n\n        var attempts: u32 = 0;\n        while (attempts < self.max_retries) : (attempts += 1) {\n            // Read generation before loading\n            const gen_before = try gen.read();\n            const wal_path = try gen.walPath(gen_before);\n            errdefer self.allocator.free(wal_path);\n\n            // Read generation after loading\n            const gen_after = try gen.read();\n\n            if (gen_before == gen_after) {\n                // Generation stable - return consistent state\n                return LoadResult{\n                    .generation = gen_before,\n                    .wal_path = wal_path,\n                    .retried = retried,\n                };\n            }\n\n            // Generation changed during read - retry\n            self.allocator.free(wal_path);\n            retried = true;\n        }\n\n        // Max retries exceeded - return latest generation\n        // (this should be very rare, only under extreme compaction load)\n        const final_gen = try gen.read();\n        return LoadResult{\n            .generation = final_gen,\n            .wal_path = try gen.walPath(final_gen),\n            .retried = retried,\n        };\n    }\n};\n\n// --- Tests ---\n\ntest \"Generation.read returns MIN_GENERATION for missing file\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"gen_missing\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    var gen = Generation.init(test_dir, allocator);\n    const value = try gen.read();\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u64, 1), value);\n}\n\ntest \"Generation.write and read roundtrip\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u64, 123456789), value2);\n}\n\ntest \"Generation.walPath generates correct paths\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n\n    var gen = Generation.init(\".beads\", allocator);\n\n    const path1 = try gen.walPath(1);\n    defer allocator.free(path1);\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\".beads/beads.wal.1\", path1);\n\n    const path2 = try gen.walPath(42);\n    defer allocator.free(path2);\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\".beads/beads.wal.42\", path2);\n}\n\ntest \"GenerationAwareLoader.getConsistentGeneration Write-Ahead Log (WAL) for beads_zig.\n     2→//!\n     3→//! Provides constant-time concurrent writes by appending operations to a WAL file\n     4→//! rather than rewriting the entire main JSONL file. Operations are:\n     5→//! - Serialized via flock before append\n     6→//! - fsync'd before lock release for durability\n     7→//! - Replayed on read to reconstruct current state\n     8→//!\n     9→//! WAL entry format (binary framed):\n    10→//!   [magic:u32][crc:u32][len:u32][json_payload][newline]\n    11→//!\n    12→//! - magic: 0xB3AD5 - enables quick validation of WAL integrity\n    13→//! - crc: CRC32 checksum of the JSON payload (detects corruption)\n    14→//! - len: length of JSON payload (enables skipping without parsing)\n    15→//! - json_payload: the actual WAL entry as JSON\n    16→//! - newline: \\n for human readability when inspecting\n    17→//!\n    18→//! Legacy format (plain JSON lines) is also supported for reading:\n    19→//! {\"op\":\"add\",\"ts\":1706540000,\"id\":\"bd-abc123\",\"data\":{...}}\n    20→//!\n    21→//! Generation numbers prevent read/compact races:\n    22→//! - Each compaction rotates to a new generation (beads.wal.N -> beads.wal.N+1)\n    23→//! - Readers check generation before/after read and retry if changed\n    24→//! - Old WAL files cleaned up after successful compaction\n    25→\n    26→const std = @import(\"std\");\n    27→const fs = std.fs;\n    28→const Issue = @import(\"../models/issue.zig\").Issue;\n    29→const BeadsLock = @import(\"lock.zig\").BeadsLock;\n    30→const IssueStore = @import(\"store.zig\").IssueStore;\n    31→const Generation = @import(\"generation.zig\").Generation;\n    32→const GenerationAwareLoader = @import(\"generation.zig\").GenerationAwareLoader;\n    33→const test_util = @import(\"../test_util.zig\");\n    34→\n    35→/// Magic bytes to identify framed WAL entries: 0x000B3AD5 (\"BEADS\" in hex-ish)\n    36→pub const WAL_MAGIC: u32 = 0x000B3AD5;\n    37→\n    38→/// Size of the binary frame header (magic + crc + len)\n    39→pub const FRAME_HEADER_SIZE: usize = 12;\n    40→\n    41→pub const WalError = error{\n    42→    WalCorrupted,\n    43→    WriteError,\n    44→    LockFailed,\n    45→    InvalidOperation,\n    46→    ParseError,\n    47→    OutOfMemory,\n    48→    ReplayPartialFailure,\n    49→    ChecksumMismatch,\n    50→};\n    51→\n    52→/// Statistics from WAL replay operations.\n    53→pub const ReplayStats = struct {\n    54→    applied: usize = 0,\n    55→    skipped: usize = 0,\n    56→    failed: usize = 0,\n    57→    failure_ids: []const []const u8 = &.{},\n    58→\n    59→    pub fn deinit(self: *ReplayStats, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) void {\n    60→        for (self.failure_ids) |id| {\n    61→            allocator.free(id);\n    62→        }\n    63→        if (self.failure_ids.len > 0) {\n    64→            allocator.free(self.failure_ids);\n    65→        }\n    66→    }\n    67→\n    68→    pub fn hasFailures(self: ReplayStats) bool {\n    69→        return self.failed > 0;\n    70→    }\n    71→};\n    72→\n    73→/// WAL operation types.\n    74→pub const WalOp = enum {\n    75→    add,\n    76→    update,\n    77→    close,\n    78→    reopen,\n    79→    delete,\n    80→    set_blocked,\n    81→    unset_blocked,\n    82→\n    83→    pub fn toString(self: WalOp) []const u8 {\n    84→        return switch (self) {\n    85→            .add => \"add\",\n    86→            .update => \"update\",\n    87→            .close => \"close\",\n    88→            .reopen => \"reopen\",\n    89→            .delete => \"delete\",\n    90→            .set_blocked => \"set_blocked\",\n    91→            .unset_blocked => \"unset_blocked\",\n    92→        };\n    93→    }\n    94→\n    95→    pub fn fromString(s: []const u8) ?WalOp {\n    96→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, s, \"add\")) return .add;\n    97→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, s, \"update\")) return .update;\n    98→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, s, \"close\")) return .close;\n    99→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, s, \"reopen\")) return .reopen;\n   100→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, s, \"delete\")) return .delete;\n   101→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, s, \"set_blocked\")) return .set_blocked;\n   102→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, s, \"unset_blocked\")) return .unset_blocked;\n   103→        return null;\n   104→    }\n   105→};\n   106→\n   107→/// A single WAL entry representing one operation.\n   108→pub const WalEntry = struct {\n   109→    op: WalOp,\n   110→    ts: i64, // Unix timestamp for ordering\n   111→    seq: u64 = 0, // Monotonic sequence number for deterministic ordering within same timestamp\n   112→    id: []const u8, // Issue ID\n   113→    data: ?Issue, // Full issue for add/update, null for status-only ops\n   114→\n   115→    const Self = @This();\n   116→\n   117→    /// Custom JSON serialization for WalEntry.\n   118→    pub fn jsonStringify(self: Self, jws: anytype) !void {\n   119→        try jws.beginObject();\n   120→\n   121→        try jws.objectField(\"op\");\n   122→        try jws.write(self.op.toString());\n   123→\n   124→        try jws.objectField(\"ts\");\n   125→        try jws.write(self.ts);\n   126→\n   127→        try jws.objectField(\"seq\");\n   128→        try jws.write(self.seq);\n   129→\n   130→        try jws.objectField(\"id\");\n   131→        try jws.write(self.id);\n   132→\n   133→        try jws.objectField(\"data\");\n   134→        if (self.data) |issue| {\n   135→            try jws.write(issue);\n   136→        } else {\n   137→            try jws.write(null);\n   138→        }\n   139→\n   140→        try jws.endObject();\n   141→    }\n   142→};\n   143→\n   144→/// Parsed WAL entry for replay.\n   145→pub const ParsedWalEntry = struct {\n   146→    op: WalOp,\n   147→    ts: i64,\n   148→    seq: u64 = 0, // Sequence number (0 for legacy entries)\n   149→    id: []const u8,\n   150→    data: ?Issue,\n   151→\n   152→    pub fn deinit(self: *ParsedWalEntry, allocator:   }\n   158→    }\n   159→};\n   160→\n   161→/// WAL file manager for reading and writing operations.\n   162→/// Supports generation-based file rotation for read/compact race safety.\n   163→pub const Wal = struct {\n   164→    beads_dir: []const u8,\n   165→    wal_path: []const u8,\n   166→    lock_path: []const u8,\n   167→    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n   168→    next_seq: u64 = 1, // Next sequence number to assign\n   169→    generation: u64 = 1, // Current generation number\n   170→    owns_wal_path: bool = true, // Whether we allocated wal_path\n   171→\n   172→    const Self = @This();\n   173→\n   174→    /// Initialize WAL with generation-aware path.\n   175→    /// Reads current generation from disk and uses appropriate WAL file.\n   176→    pub fn init(beads_dir: []const u8, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) !Self {\n   177→        // Read current generation\n   178→        var gen = Generation.init(beads_dir, allocator);\n   179→        const current_gen = gen.read() catch 1;\n   180→\n   181→        // Build generation-aware WAL path\n   182→        const wal_path = try gen.walPath(current_gen);\n   183→        errdefer allocator.free(wal_path);\n   184→\n   185→        const lock_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ beads_dir, \"beads.lock\" });\n   186→        errdefer allocator.free(lock_path);\n   187→\n   188→        const beads_dir_copy = try allocator.dupe(u8, beads_dir);\n   189→\n   190→        return Self{\n   191→            .beads_dir = beads_dir_copy,\n   192→            .wal_path = wal_path,\n   193→            .lock_path = lock_path,\n   194→            .allocator = allocator,\n   195→            .next_seq = 1,\n   196→            .generation = current_gen,\n   197→            .owns_wal_path = true,\n   198→        };\n   199→    }\n   200→\n   201→    /// Initialize WAL with a specific path (for testing or direct path usage).\n   202→    /// Does not use generation-aware paths.\n   203→    pub fn initWithPath(wal_path: []const u8, lock_path: []const u8, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) Self {\n   204→        return Self{\n   205→            .beads_dir = \"\",\n   206→            .wal_path = wal_path,\n   207→            .lock_path = lock_path,\n   208→            .allocator = allocator,\n   209→            .next_seq = 1,\n   210→            .generation = 1,\n   211→            .owns_wal_path = false,\n   212→        };\n   213→    }\n   214→\n   215→    pub fn deinit(self: *Self) void {\n   216→        if (self.owns_wal_path) {\n   217→            self.allocator.free(self.wal_path);\n   218→        }\n   219→        self.allocator.free(self.lock_path);\n   220→        if (self.beads_dir.len > 0) {\n   221→            self.allocator.free(self.beads_dir);\n   222→        }\n   223→    }\n   224→\n   225→    /// Get current generation number.\n   226→    pub fn getGeneration(self: *Self) u64 {\n   227→        return self.generation;\n   228→    }\n   229→\n   230→    /// Refresh generation from disk and update WAL path if changed.\n   231→    /// Call this before reading to ensure we're using the latest generation.\n   232→    pub fn refreshGeneration(self: *Self) !bool {\n   233→        if (self.beads_dir.len == 0) return false; // Not using generation-aware paths\n   234→\n   235→        var gen = Generation.init(self.beads_dir, self.allocator);\n   236→        const current_gen = gen.read() catch return false;\n   237→\n   238→        if (current_gen != self.generation) {\n   239→            // Generation changed - update WAL path\n   240→            const new_wal_path = try gen.walPath(current_gen);\n   241→\n   242→            if (self.owns_wal_path) {\n   243→                self.allocator.free(self.wal_path);\n   244→            }\n   245→            self.wal_path = new_wal_path;\n   246→            self.owns_wal_path = true;\n   247→            self.generation = current_gen;\n   248→            return true;\n   249→        }\n   250→        return false;\n   251→    }\n   252→\n   253→    /// Rotate to a new generation (used by compactor).\n   254→    /// Creates a new WAL file and returns the new generation number.\n   255→    /// IMPORTANT: Caller must already hold the exclusive lock.\n   256→    pub fn rotateGeneration(self: *Self) !u64 {\n   257→        if (self.beads_dir.len == 0) return self.generation;\n   258→\n   259→        var gen = Generation.init(self.beads_dir, self.allocator);\n   260→        // Use incrementUnlocked since caller (compact) already holds the lock\n   261→        const new_gen = try gen.incrementUnlocked();\n   262→\n   263→        // Update our WAL path to the new generation\n   264→        const new_wal_path = try gen.walPath(new_gen);\n   265→\n   266→        if (self.owns_wal_path) {\n   267→            self.allocator.free(self.wal_path);\n   268→        }\n   269→        self.wal_path = new_wal_path;\n   270→        self.owns_wal_path = true;\n   271→        self.generation = new_gen;\n   272→\n   273→        // Clean up old generations (keep current and previous)\n   274→        gen.cleanupOldGenerations(new_gen);\n   275→\n   276→        return new_gen;\n   277→    }\n   278→\n   279→    /// Load the next sequence number from existing WAL entries.\n   280→    /// Call this after init to ensure sequence numbers are unique.\n   281→    pub fn loadNextSeq(self: *Self) !void {\n   282→        const entries = self.readEntries() catch return;\n   283→        defer {\n   284→            for (entries) |*e| {\n   285→                var entry = e.*;\n   286→                entry.deinit(self.allocator);\n   287→            }\n   288→            self.allocator.free(entries);\n   289→        }\n   290→\n   291→        var max_seq: u64 = 0;\n   292→        for (entries) |e| {\n   293→            if (e.seq > max_seq) max_seq = e.seq;\n   294→        }\n   295→        self.next_seq = max_seq + 1;\n   296→    }\n   297→\n   298→    /// Append an entry to the WAL under exclusive lock.\n   299→    /// Ensures durability via fsync before releasing lock.\n   300→    /// Assigns a monotonic sequence number to the entry.\n   301→    pub fn appendEntry(self: *Self, entry: WalEntry) !void {\n   302→        var lock = BeadsLock.acquire(self.lock_path) catch return WalError.LockFailed;\n   303→        defer lock.release();\n   304→\n   305→        // Assign sequence number under lock\n   306→        var entry_with_seq = entry;\n   307→        entry_with_seq.seq = self.next_seq;\n   308→        self.next_seq += 1;\n   309→\n   310→        try self.appendEntryUnlocked(entry_with_seq);\n   311→    }\n   312→\n   313→    /// Append entry without acquiring lock (caller must hold lock).\n   314→    fn appendEntryUnlocked(self: *Self, entry: WalEntry) !void {\n   315→        const dir = fs.cwd();\n   316→\n   317→        // Ensure parent directory exists\n   318→        if (std.fs.path.dirname(self.wal_path)) |parent| {\n   319→            dir.makePath(parent) catch |err| switch (err) {\n   320→                error.PathAlreadyExists => {},\n   321→                else => return err,\n   322→            };\n   323→        }\n   324→\n   325→        // Open or create WAL file in append mode\n   326→        const file = dir.createFile(self.wal_path, .{\n   327→            .truncate = false,\n   328→        }) catch return WalError.WriteError;\n   329→        defer file.close();\n   330→\n   331→        // Seek to end\n   332→        file.seekFromEnd(0) catch return WalError.WriteError;\n   333→\n   334→        // Serialize entry to JSON\n   335→        const json_bytes = std.json.Stringify.valueAlloc(self.allocator, entry, .{}) catch return WalError.WriteError;\n   336→        defer self.allocator.free(json_bytes);\n   337→\n   338→        // Compute CRC32 checksum of the JSON payload\n   339→        const crc = std.hash.Crc32.hash(json_bytes);\n   340→\n   341→        // Write binary frame header: [magic:u32][crc:u32][len:u32]\n   342→        const len: u32 = @intCast(json_bytes.len);\n   343→        var header: [FRAME_HEADER_SIZE]u8 = undefined;\n   344→        std.mem.writeInt(u32, header[0..4], WAL_MAGIC, .little);\n   345→        std.mem.writeInt(u32, header[4..8], crc, .little);\n   346→        std.mem.writeInt(u32, header[8..12], len, .little);\n   347→\n   348→        file.writeAll(&header) catch return WalError.WriteError;\n   349→        file.writeAll(json_bytes) catch return WalError.WriteError;\n   350→        file.writeAll(\"\\n\") catch return WalError.WriteError;\n   351→\n   352→        // fsync for durability\n   353→        file.sync() catch return WalError.WriteError;\n   354→    }\n   355→\n   356→    /// Read all WAL entries with generation-aware consistency checking.\n   357→    /// Supports both framed format (with CRC32) and legacy plain JSON lines.\n   358→    /// If generation changes during read (compaction occurred), retries with new generation.\n   359→    pub fn readEntries(self: *Self) ![]ParsedWalEntry {\n   360→        // If using generation-aware paths, check for consistency\n   361→        if (self.beads_dir.len > 0) {\n   362→            return self.readEntriesWithGenerationCheck();\n   363→        }\n   364→        return self.readEntriesFromPath(self.wal_path);\n   365→    }\n   366→\n   367→    /// Read entries with generation consistency checking.\n   368→    /// Retries up to 3 times if generation changes during read.\n   369→    fn readEntriesWithGenerationCheck(self: *Self) ![]ParsedWalEntry {\n   370→        var gen = Generation.init(self.beads_dir, self.allocator);\n   371→        const max_retries: u32 = 3;\n   372→        var attempts: u32 = 0;\n   373→\n   374→        while (attempts < max_retries) : (attempts += 1) {\n   375→            // Read generation before loading\n   376→            const gen_before = gen.read() catch self.generation;\n   377→\n   378→            // Get WAL path for this generation\n   379→            const wal_path = try gen.walPath(gen_before);\n   380→            defer self.allocator.free(wal_path);\n   381→\n   382→            // Read entries\n   383→            const entries = try self.readEntriesFromPath(wal_path);\n   384→\n   385→            // Read generation after loading\n   386→            const gen_after = gen.read() catch gen_before;\n   387→\n   388→            if (gen_before == gen_after) {\n   389→                // Generation stable - return consistent state\n   390→                // Update our cached generation\n   391→                if (gen_before != self.generation) {\n   392→                    if (self.owns_wal_path) {\n   393→                        self.allocator.free(self.wal_path);\n   394→                    }\n   395→                    self.wal_path = try gen.walPath(gen_before);\n   396→                    self.owns_wal_path = true;\n   397→                    self.generation = gen_before;\n   398→                }\n   399→                return entries;\n   400→            }\n   401→\n   402→            // Generation changed during read - free entries and retry\n   403→            for (entries) |*e| {\n   404→                var entry = e.*;\n   405→                entry.deinit(self.allocator);\n   406→            }\n   407→            self.allocator.free(entries);\n   408→        }\n   409→\n   410→        // Max retries exceeded - return latest generation's entries\n   411→        const final_gen = gen.read() catch self.generation;\n   412→        const final_path = try gen.walPath(final_gen);\n   413→        defer self.allocator.free(final_path);\n   414→        return self.readEntriesFromPath(final_path);\n   415→    }\n   416→\n   417→    /// Read entries from a specific WAL file path.\n   418→    fn readEntriesFromPath(self: *Self, path: []const u8) ![]ParsedWalEntry {\n   419→        const file = fs.cwd().openFile(path, .{}) catch |err| switch (err) {\n   420→            error.FileNotFound => return &[_]ParsedWalEntry{},\n   421→            else => return err,\n   422→        };\n   423→        defer file.close();\n   424→\n   425→        const content = file.readToEndAlloc(self.allocator, 100 * 1024 * 1024) catch return WalError.ParseError;\n   426→        defer self.allocator.free(content);\n   427→\n   428→        var entries: std.ArrayListUnmanaged(ParsedWalEntry) = .{};\n   429→        errdefer {\n   430→            for (entries.items) |*e| {\n   431→                e.deinit(self.allocator);\n   432→            }\n   433→            entries.deinit(self.allocator);\n   434→        }\n   435→\n   436→        var pos: usize = 0;\n   437→        while (pos < content.len) {\n   438→            // Try to parse as framed entry first (check for magic bytes)\n   439→            if (pos + FRAME_HEADER_SIZE <= content.len) {\n   440→                const magic = std.mem.readInt(u32, content[pos..][0..4], .little);\n   441→                if (magic == WAL_MAGIC) {\n   442→                    // Framed format: [magic:u32][crc:u32][len:u32][json][newline]\n   443→                    const stored_crc = std.mem.readInt(u32, content[pos + 4 ..][0..4], .little);\n   444→                    const len = std.mem.readInt(u32, content[pos + 8 ..][0..4], .little);\n   445→\n   446→                    const payload_start = pos + FRAME_HEADER_SIZE;\n   447→                    const payload_end = payload_start + len;\n   448→\n   449→                    // Check for truncation\n   450→                    if (payload_end > content.len) {\n   451→                        // Truncated entry - skip to end (partial write from crash)\n   452→                        break;\n   453→                    }\n   454→\n   455→                    const json_payload = content[payload_start..payload_end];\n   456→\n   457→                    // Verify CRC32\n   458→                    const computed_crc = std.hash.Crc32.hash(json_payload);\n   459→                    if (computed_crc != stored_crc) {\n   460→                        // CRC mismatch - corrupted entry, skip it\n   461→                        // Try to find next entry by looking for next magic or newline\n   462→                        pos = payload_end;\n   463→                        if (pos < content.len and content[pos] == '\\n') {\n   464→                            pos += 1;\n   465→                        }\n   466→                        continue;\n   467→                    }\n   468→\n   469→                    // Parse the JSON payload\n   470→                    if (self.parseEntry(json_payload)) |entry| {\n   471→                        try entries.append(self.allocator, entry);\n   472→                    } else |_| {\n   473→                        // JSON parse error - skip\n   474→                    }\n   475→\n   476→                    // Move past the entry (json + newline)\n   477→                    pos = payload_end;\n   478→                    if (pos < content.len and content[pos] == '\\n') {\n   479→                        pos += 1;\n   480→                    }\n   481→                    continue;\n   482→                }\n   483→            }\n   484→\n   485→            // Fall back to legacy plain JSON line format\n   486→            // Find the next newline\n   487→            var line_end = pos;\n   488→            while (line_end < content.len and content[line_end] != '\\n') {\n   489→                line_end += 1;\n   490→            }\n   491→\n   492→            if (line_end > pos) {\n   493→                const line = content[pos..line_end];\n   494→                if (self.parseEntry(line)) |entry| {\n   495→                    try entries.append(self.allocator, entry);\n   496→                } else |_| {\n   497→                    // Skip malformed entries (graceful degradation)\n   498→                }\n   499→            }\n   500→\n   501→            pos = line_end;\n   502→            if (pos < content.len and content[pos] == '\\n') {\n   503→                pos += 1;\n   504→            }\n   505→        }\n   506→\n   507→        return entries.toOwnedSlice(self.allocator);\n   508→    }\n   509→\n   510→    /// Parse a single WAL entry line.\n   511→    fn parseEntry(self: *Self, line: []const u8) !ParsedWalEntry {\n   512→        const parsed = std.json.parseFromSlice(\n   513→            struct {\n   514→                op: []const u8,\n   515→                ts: i64,\n   516→                seq: u64 = 0, // Default to 0 for legacy entries without seq\n   517→                id: []const u8,\n   518→                data: ?Issue,\n   519→            },\n   520→            self.allocator,\n   521→            line,\n   522→            .{ .ignore_unknown_fields = true, .allocate = .alloc_always },\n   523→        ) catch return WalError.ParseError;\n   524→        defer parsed.deinit();\n   525→\n   526→        const op = WalOp.fromString(parsed.value.op) orelse return WalError.InvalidOperation;\n   527→\n   528→        // Clone strings since parsed will be freed\n   529→        const id = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, parsed.value.id);\n   530→        errdefer self.allocator.free(id);\n   531→\n   532→        var data: ?Issue = null;\n   533→        if (parsed.value.data) |issue| {\n   534→            data = try issue.clone(self.allocator);\n   535→        }\n   536→\n   537→        return ParsedWalEntry{\n   538→            .op = op,\n   539→            .ts = parsed.value.ts,\n   540→            .seq = parsed.value.seq,\n   541→            .id = id,\n   542→            .data = data,\n   543→        };\n   544→    }\n   545→\n   546→    /// Replay WAL entries onto an IssueStore.\n   547→    /// Applies operations in timestamp/sequence order.\n   548→    /// Returns statistics about the replay including any failures.\n   549→    pub fn replay(self: *Self, store: *IssueStore) !ReplayStats {\n   550→        const entries = try self.readEntries();\n   551→        defer {\n   552→            for (entries) |*e| {\n   553→                var entry = e.*;\n   554→                entry.deinit(self.allocator);\n   555→            }\n   556→            self.allocator.free(entries);\n   557→        }\n   558→\n   559→        // Sort by timestamp, then by sequence number for deterministic ordering\n   560→        // when multiple entries have the same timestamp\n   561→        std.mem.sortUnstable(ParsedWalEntry, @constCast(entries), {}, struct {\n   562→            fn lessThan(_: void, a: ParsedWalEntry, b: ParsedWalEntry) bool {\n   563→                if (a.ts != b.ts) return a.ts < b.ts;\n   564→                return a.seq < b.seq;\n   565→            }\n   566→        }.lessThan);\n   567→\n   568→        // Track replay results\n   569→        var stats = ReplayStats{};\n   570→        var failure_ids: std.ArrayListUnmanaged([]const u8) = .{};\n   571→        errdefer {\n   572→            for (failure_ids.items) |id| {\n   573→                self.allocator.free(id);\n   574→            }\n   575→            failure_ids.deinit(self.allocator);\n   576→        }\n   577→\n   578→        // Apply each operation\n   579→        for (entries) |entry| {\n   580→            const result = self.applyEntry(store, entry);\n   581→            switch (result) {\n   582→                .applied => stats.applied += 1,\n   583→                .skipped => stats.skipped += 1,\n   584→                .failed => {\n   585→                    stats.failed += 1;\n   586→                    const id_copy = self.allocator.dupe(u8, entry.id) catch continue;\n   587→                    failure_ids.append(self.allocator, id_copy) catch {\n   588→                        self.allocator.free(id_copy);\n   589→                    };\n   590→                },\n   591→            }\n   592→        }\n   593→\n   594→        stats.failure_ids = failure_ids.toOwnedSlice(self.allocator) catch &.{};\n   595→        return stats;\n   596→    }\n   597→\n   598→    /// Result of applying a single WAL entry.\n   599→    const ApplyResult = enum {\n   600→        applied,\n   601→        skipped,\n   602→        failed,\n   603→    };\n   604→\n   605→    /// Apply a single WAL entry to the store.\n   606→    /// Returns the result of the operation.\n   607→    fn applyEntry(self: *Self, store: *IssueStore, entry: ParsedWalEntry) ApplyResult {\n   608→        _ = self;\n   609→        switch (entry.op) {\n   610→            .add => {\n   611→                if (entry.data) |issue| {\n   612→                    // Only insert if not already present\n   613→                    if (!store.id_index.contains(issue.id)) {\n   614→                        store.insert(issue) catch |err| switch (err) {\n   615→                            error.DuplicateId => return .skipped, // Already exists\n   616→                            else => return .failed,\n   617→                        };\n   618→                        return .applied;\n   619→                    }\n   620→                    return .skipped; // Already exists\n   621→                }\n   622→                return .skipped; // No data for add op\n   623→            },\n   624→            .update => {\n   625→                if (entry.data) |issue| {\n   626→                    // Update or insert\n   627→                    if (store.id_index.contains(issue.id)) {\n   628→                        // Full replacement for simplicity\n   629→                        const idx = store.id_index.get(issue.id).?;\n   630→                        var old = &store.issues.items[idx];\n   631→                        old.deinit(store.allocator);\n   632→                        store.issues.items[idx] = issue.clone(store.allocator) catch return .failed;\n   633→                        return .applied;\n   634→                    } else {\n   635→                        store.insert(issue) catch return .failed;\n   636→                        return .applied;\n   637→                    }\n   638→                }\n   639→                return .skipped; // No data for update op\n   640→            },\n   641→            .close => {\n   642→                store.update(entry.id, .{\n   643→                    .status = .closed,\n   644→                    .closed_at = std.time.timestamp(),\n   645→                }, entry.ts) catch |err| switch (err) {\n   646→                    error.IssueNotFound => return .skipped,\n   647→                    else => return .failed,\n   648→                };\n   649→                return .applied;\n   650→            },\n   651→            .reopen => {\n   652→                store.update(entry.id, .{\n   653→                    .status = .open,\n   654→                }, entry.ts) catch |err| switch (err) {\n   655→                    error.IssueNotFound => return .skipped,\n   656→                    else => return .failed,\n   657→                };\n   658→                return .applied;\n   659→            },\n   660→            .delete => {\n   661→                store.delete(entry.id, entry.ts) catch |err| switch (err) {\n   662→                    error.IssueNotFound => return .skipped,\n   663→                    else => return .failed,\n   664→                };\n   665→                return .applied;\n   666→            },\n   667→            .set_blocked => {\n   668→                store.update(entry.id, .{ .status = .blocked }, entry.ts) catch |err| switch (err) {\n   669→                    error.IssueNotFound => return .skipped,\n   670→                    else => return .failed,\n   671→                };\n   672→                return .applied;\n   673→            },\n   674→            .unset_blocked => {\n   675→                store.update(entry.id, .{ .status = .open }, entry.ts) catch |err| switch (err) {\n   676→                    error.IssueNotFound => return .skipped,\n   677→                    else => return .failed,\n   678→                };\n   679→                return .applied;\n   680→            },\n   681→        }\n   682→    }\n   683→\n   684→    /// Get the number of entries in the WAL.\n   685→    pub fn entryCount(self: *Self) !usize {\n   686→        const entries = try self.readEntries();\n   687→        defer {\n   688→            for (entries) |*e| {\n   689→                e.deinit(self.allocator);\n   690→            }\n   691→            self.allocator.free(entries);\n   692→        }\n   693→        return entries.len;\n   694→    }\n   695→\n   696→    /// Get the size of the WAL file in bytes.\n   697→    pub fn fileSize(self: *Self) !u64 {\n   698→        const file = fs.cwd().openFile(self.wal_path, .{}) catch |err| switch (err) {\n   699→            error.FileNotFound => return 0,\n   700→            else => return err,\n   701→        };\n   702→        defer file.close();\n   703→\n   704→        const stat = try file.stat();\n   705→        return stat.size;\n   706→    }\n   707→\n   708→    /// Truncate the WAL file (used after compaction).\n   709→    pub fn truncate(self: *Self) !void {\n   710→        const dir = fs.cwd();\n   711→        dir.deleteFile(self.wal_path) catch |err| switch (err) {\n   712→            error.FileNotFound => {}, // Already empty\n   713→            else => return err,\n   714→        };\n   715→    }\n   716→\n   717→    // Convenience methods for common operations\n   718→\n   719→    /// Add a new issue to the WAL.\n   720→    pub fn addIssue(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n   721→        try self.appendEntry(.{\n   722→            .op = .add,\n   723→            .ts = std.time.timestamp(),\n   724→            .id = issue.id,\n   725→            .data = issue,\n   726→        });\n   727→    }\n   728→\n   729→    /// Close an issue in the WAL.\n   730→    pub fn closeIssue(self: *Self, id: []const u8) !void {\n   731→        try self.appendEntry(.{\n   732→            .op = .close,\n   733→            .ts = std.time.timestamp(),\n   734→            .id = id,\n   735→            .data = null,\n   736→        });\n   737→    }\n   738→\n   739→    /// Reopen an issue in the WAL.\n   740→    pub fn reopenIssue(self: *Self, id: []const u8) !void {\n   741→        try self.appendEntry(.{\n   742→            .op = .reopen,\n   743→            .ts = std.time.timestamp(),\n   744→            .id = id,\n   745→            .data = null,\n   746→        });\n   747→    }\n   748→\n   749→    /// Update an issue in the WAL.\n   750→    pub fn updateIssue(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n   751→        try self.appendEntry(.{\n   752→            .op = .update,\n   753→            .ts = std.time.timestamp(),\n   754→            .id = issue.id,\n   755→            .data = issue,\n   756→        });\n   757→    }\n   758→\n   759→    /// Delete an issue in the WAL (tombstone).\n   760→    pub fn deleteIssue(self: *Self, id: []const u8) !void {\n   761→        try
