Write-Ahead Log (WAL) for beads_zig.\n//!\n//! Provides constant-time concurrent writes by appending operations to a WAL file\n//! rather than rewriting the entire main JSONL file. Operations are:\n//! - Serialized via flock before append\n//! - fsync'd before lock release for durability\n//! - Replayed on read to reconstruct current state\n//!\n//! WAL entry format (binary framed):\n//!   [magic:u32][crc:u32][len:u32][json_payload][newline]\n//!\n//! - magic: 0xB3AD5 - enables quick validation of WAL integrity\n//! - crc: CRC32 checksum of the JSON payload (detects corruption)\n//! - len: length of JSON payload (enables skipping without parsing)\n//! - json_payload: the actual WAL entry as JSON\n//! - newline: \\n for human readability when inspecting\n//!\n//! Legacy format (plain JSON lines) is also supported for reading:\n//! {\"op\":\"add\",\"ts\":1706540000,\"id\":\"bd-abc123\",\"data\":{...}}\n//!\n//! Generation numbers prevent read/compact races:\n//! - Each compaction rotates to a new generation (beads.wal.N -> beads.wal.N+1)\n//! - Readers check generation before/after read and retry if changed\n//! - Old WAL files cleaned up after successful compaction\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\nconst fs = std.fs;\nconst Issue = @import(\"../models/issue.zig\").Issue;\nconst BeadsLock = @import(\"lock.zig\").BeadsLock;\nconst IssueStore = @import(\"store.zig\").IssueStore;\nconst Generation = @import(\"generation.zig\").Generation;\nconst GenerationAwareLoader = @import(\"generation.zig\").GenerationAwareLoader;\nconst test_util = @import(\"../test_util.zig\");\n\n/// Magic bytes to identify framed WAL entries: 0x000B3AD5 (\"BEADS\" in hex-ish)\npub const WAL_MAGIC: u32 = 0x000B3AD5;\n\n/// Size of the binary frame header (magic + crc + len)\npub const FRAME_HEADER_SIZE: usize = 12;\n\npub const WalError = error{\n    WalCorrupted,\n    WriteError,\n    LockFailed,\n    InvalidOperation,\n    ParseError,\n    OutOfMemory,\n    ReplayPartialFailure,\n    ChecksumMismatch,\n};\n\n/// Statistics from WAL replay operations.\npub const ReplayStats = struct {\n    applied: usize = 0,\n    skipped: usize = 0,\n    failed: usize = 0,\n    failure_ids: []const []const u8 = &.{},\n\n    pub fn deinit(self: *ReplayStats, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) void {\n        for (self.failure_ids) |id| {\n            allocator.free(id);\n        }\n        if (self.failure_ids.len > 0) {\n            allocator.free(self.failure_ids);\n        }\n    }\n\n    pub fn hasFailures(self: ReplayStats) bool {\n        return self.failed > 0;\n    }\n};\n\n/// WAL operation types.\npub const WalOp = enum {\n    add,\n    update,\n    close,\n    reopen,\n    delete,\n    set_blocked,\n    unset_blocked,\n\n    pub fn toString(self: WalOp) []const u8 {\n        return switch (self) {\n            .add => \"add\",\n            .update => \"update\",\n            .close => \"close\",\n            .reopen => \"reopen\",\n            .delete => \"delete\",\n            .set_blocked => \"set_blocked\",\n            .unset_blocked => \"unset_blocked\",\n        };\n    }\n\n    pub fn fromString(s: []const u8) ?WalOp {\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, s, \"add\")) return .add;\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, s, \"update\")) return .update;\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, s, \"close\")) return .close;\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, s, \"reopen\")) return .reopen;\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, s, \"delete\")) return .delete;\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, s, \"set_blocked\")) return .set_blocked;\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, s, \"unset_blocked\")) return .unset_blocked;\n        return null;\n    }\n};\n\n/// A single WAL entry representing one operation.\npub const WalEntry = struct {\n    op: WalOp,\n    ts: i64, // Unix timestamp for ordering\n    seq: u64 = 0, // Monotonic sequence number for deterministic ordering within same timestamp\n    id: []const u8, // Issue ID\n    data: ?Issue, // Full issue for add/update, null for status-only ops\n\n    const Self = @This();\n\n    /// Custom JSON serialization for WalEntry.\n    pub fn jsonStringify(self: Self, jws: anytype) !void {\n        try jws.beginObject();\n\n        try jws.objectField(\"op\");\n        try jws.write(self.op.toString());\n\n        try jws.objectField(\"ts\");\n        try jws.write(self.ts);\n\n        try jws.objectField(\"seq\");\n        try jws.write(self.seq);\n\n        try jws.objectField(\"id\");\n        try jws.write(self.id);\n\n        try jws.objectField(\"data\");\n        if (self.data) |issue| {\n            try jws.write(issue);\n        } else {\n            try jws.write(null);\n        }\n\n        try jws.endObject();\n    }\n};\n\n/// Parsed WAL entry for replay.\npub const ParsedWalEntry = struct {\n    op: WalOp,\n    ts: i64,\n    seq: u64 = 0, // Sequence number (0 for legacy entries)\n    id: []const u8,\n    data: ?Issue,\n\n    pub fn deinit(self: *ParsedWalEntry, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) void {\n        allocator.free(self.id);\n        if (self.data) |*issue| {\n            var i = issue.*;\n            i.deinit(allocator);\n        }\n    }\n};\n\n/// WAL file manager for reading and writing operations.\n/// Supports generation-based file rotation for read/compact race safety.\npub const Wal = struct {\n    beads_dir: []const u8,\n    wal_path: []const u8,\n    lock_path: []const u8,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    next_seq: u64 = 1, // Next sequence number to assign\n    generation: u64 = 1, // Current generation number\n    owns_wal_path: bool = true, // Whether we allocated wal_path\n\n    const Self = @This();\n\n    /// Initialize WAL with generation-aware path.\n    /// Reads current generation from disk and uses appropriate WAL file.\n    pub fn init(beads_dir: []const u8, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) !Self {\n        // Read current generation\n        var gen = Generation.init(beads_dir, allocator);\n        const current_gen = gen.read() catch 1;\n\n        // Build generation-aware WAL path\n        const wal_path = try gen.walPath(current_gen);\n        errdefer allocator.free(wal_path);\n\n        const lock_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ beads_dir, \"beads.lock\" });\n        errdefer allocator.free(lock_path);\n\n        const beads_dir_copy = try allocator.dupe(u8, beads_dir);\n\n        return Self{\n            .beads_dir = beads_dir_copy,\n            .wal_path = wal_path,\n            .lock_path = lock_path,\n            .allocator = allocator,\n            .next_seq = 1,\n            .generation = current_gen,\n            .owns_wal_path = true,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Initialize WAL with a specific path (for testing or direct path usage).\n    /// Does not use generation-aware paths.\n    pub fn initWithPath(wal_path: []const u8, lock_path: []const u8, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) Self {\n        return Self{\n            .beads_dir = \"\",\n            .wal_path = wal_path,\n            .lock_path = lock_path,\n            .allocator = allocator,\n            .next_seq = 1,\n            .generation = 1,\n            .owns_wal_path = false,\n        };\n    }\n\n    pub fn deinit(self: *Self) void {\n        if (self.owns_wal_path) {\n            self.allocator.free(self.wal_path);\n        }\n        self.allocator.free(self.lock_path);\n        if (self.beads_dir.len > 0) {\n            self.allocator.free(self.beads_dir);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Get current generation number.\n    pub fn getGeneration(self: *Self) u64 {\n        return self.generation;\n    }\n\n    /// Refresh generation from disk and update WAL path if changed.\n    /// Call this before reading to ensure we're using the latest generation.\n    pub fn refreshGeneration(self: *Self) !bool {\n        if (self.beads_dir.len == 0) return false; // Not using generation-aware paths\n\n        var gen = Generation.init(self.beads_dir, self.allocator);\n        const current_gen = gen.read() catch return false;\n\n        if (current_gen != self.generation) {\n            // Generation changed - update WAL path\n            const new_wal_path = try gen.walPath(current_gen);\n\n            if (self.owns_wal_path) {\n                self.allocator.free(self.wal_path);\n            }\n            self.wal_path = new_wal_path;\n            self.owns_wal_path = true;\n            self.generation = current_gen;\n            return true;\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /// Rotate to a new generation (used by compactor).\n    /// Creates a new WAL file and returns the new generation number.\n    /// IMPORTANT: Caller must already hold the exclusive lock.\n    pub fn rotateGeneration(self: *Self) !u64 {\n        if (self.beads_dir.len == 0) return self.generation;\n\n        var gen = Generation.init(self.beads_dir, self.allocator);\n        // Use incrementUnlocked since caller (compact) already holds the lock\n        const new_gen = try gen.incrementUnlocked();\n\n        // Update our WAL path to the new generation\n        const new_wal_path = try gen.walPath(new_gen);\n\n        if (self.owns_wal_path) {\n            self.allocator.free(self.wal_path);\n        }\n        self.wal_path = new_wal_path;\n        self.owns_wal_path = true;\n        self.generation = new_gen;\n\n        // Clean up old generations (keep current and previous)\n        gen.cleanupOldGenerations(new_gen);\n\n        return new_gen;\n    }\n\n    /// Load the next sequence number from existing WAL entries.\n    /// Call this after init to ensure sequence numbers are unique.\n    pub fn loadNextSeq(self: *Self) !void {\n        const entries = self.readEntries() catch return;\n        defer {\n            for (entries) |*e| {\n                var entry = e.*;\n                entry.deinit(self.allocator);\n            }\n            self.allocator.free(entries);\n        }\n\n        var max_seq: u64 = 0;\n        for (entries) |e| {\n            if (e.seq > max_seq) max_seq = e.seq;\n        }\n        self.next_seq = max_seq + 1;\n    }\n\n    /// Append an entry to the WAL under exclusive lock.\n    /// Ensures durability via fsync before releasing lock.\n    /// Assigns a monotonic sequence number to the entry.\n    pub fn appendEntry(self: *Self, entry: WalEntry) !void {\n        var lock = BeadsLock.acquire(self.lock_path) catch return WalError.LockFailed;\n        defer lock.release();\n\n        // Assign sequence number under lock\n        var entry_with_seq = entry;\n        entry_with_seq.seq = self.next_seq;\n        self.next_seq += 1;\n\n        try self.appendEntryUnlocked(entry_with_seq);\n    }\n\n    /// Append entry without acquiring lock (caller must hold lock).\n    fn appendEntryUnlocked(self: *Self, entry: WalEntry) !void {\n        const dir = fs.cwd();\n\n        // Ensure parent directory exists\n        if (std.fs.path.dirname(self.wal_path)) |parent| {\n            dir.makePath(parent) catch |err| switch (err) {\n                error.PathAlreadyExists => {},\n                else => return err,\n            };\n        }\n\n        // Open or create WAL file in append mode\n        const file = dir.createFile(self.wal_path, .{\n            .truncate = false,\n        }) catch return WalError.WriteError;\n        defer file.close();\n\n        // Seek to end\n        file.seekFromEnd(0) catch return WalError.WriteError;\n\n        // Serialize entry to JSON\n        const json_bytes = std.json.Stringify.valueAlloc(self.allocator, entry, .{}) catch return WalError.WriteError;\n        defer self.allocator.free(json_bytes);\n\n        // Compute CRC32 checksum of the JSON payload\n        const crc = std.hash.Crc32.hash(json_bytes);\n\n        // Write binary frame header: [magic:u32][crc:u32][len:u32]\n        const len: u32 = @intCast(json_bytes.len);\n        var header: [FRAME_HEADER_SIZE]u8 = undefined;\n        std.mem.writeInt(u32, header[0..4], WAL_MAGIC, .little);\n        std.mem.writeInt(u32, header[4..8], crc, .little);\n        std.mem.writeInt(u32, header[8..12], len, .little);\n\n        file.writeAll(&header) catch return WalError.WriteError;\n        file.writeAll(json_bytes) catch return WalError.WriteError;\n        file.writeAll(\"\\n\") catch return WalError.WriteError;\n\n        // fsync for durability\n        file.sync() catch return WalError.WriteError;\n    }\n\n    /// Read all WAL entries with generation-aware consistency checking.\n    /// Supports both framed format (with CRC32) and legacy plain JSON lines.\n    /// If generation changes during read (compaction occurred), retries with new generation.\n    pub fn readEntries(self: *Self) ![]ParsedWalEntry {\n        // If using generation-aware paths, check for consistency\n        if (self.beads_dir.len > 0) {\n            return self.readEntriesWithGenerationCheck();\n        }\n        return self.readEntriesFromPath(self.wal_path);\n    }\n\n    /// Read entries with generation consistency checking.\n    /// Retries up to 3 times if generation changes during read.\n    fn readEntriesWithGenerationCheck(self: *Self) ![]ParsedWalEntry {\n        var gen = Generation.init(self.beads_dir, self.allocator);\n        const max_retries: u32 = 3;\n        var attempts: u32 = 0;\n\n        while (attempts < max_retries) : (attempts += 1) {\n            // Read generation before loading\n            const gen_before = gen.read() catch self.generation;\n\n            // Get WAL path for this generation\n            const wal_path = try gen.walPath(gen_before);\n            defer self.allocator.free(wal_path);\n\n            // Read entries\n            const entries = try self.readEntriesFromPath(wal_path);\n\n            // Read generation after loading\n            const gen_after = gen.read() catch gen_before;\n\n            if (gen_before == gen_after) {\n                // Generation stable - return consistent state\n                // Update our cached generation\n                if (gen_before != self.generation) {\n                    if (self.owns_wal_path) {\n                        self.allocator.free(self.wal_path);\n                    }\n                    self.wal_path = try gen.walPath(gen_before);\n                    self.owns_wal_path = true;\n                    self.generation = gen_before;\n                }\n                return entries;\n            }\n\n            // Generation changed during read - free entries and retry\n            for (entries) |*e| {\n                var entry = e.*;\n                entry.deinit(self.allocator);\n            }\n            self.allocator.free(entries);\n        }\n\n        // Max retries exceeded - return latest generation's entries\n        const final_gen = gen.read() catch self.generation;\n        const final_path = try gen.walPath(final_gen);\n        defer self.allocator.free(final_path);\n        return self.readEntriesFromPath(final_path);\n    }\n\n    /// Read entries from a specific WAL file path.\n    fn readEntriesFromPath(self: *Self, path: []const u8) ![]ParsedWalEntry {\n        const file = fs.cwd().openFile(path, .{}) catch |err| switch (err) {\n            error.FileNotFound => return &[_]ParsedWalEntry{},\n            else => return err,\n        };\n        defer file.close();\n\n        const content = file.readToEndAlloc(self.allocator, 100 * 1024 * 1024) catch return WalError.ParseError;\n        defer self.allocator.free(content);\n\n        var entries: std.ArrayListUnmanaged(ParsedWalEntry) = .{};\n        errdefer {\n            for (entries.items) |*e| {\n                e.deinit(self.allocator);\n            }\n            entries.deinit(self.allocator);\n        }\n\n        var pos: usize = 0;\n        while (pos < content.len) {\n            // Try to parse as framed entry first (check for magic bytes)\n            if (pos + FRAME_HEADER_SIZE <= content.len) {\n                const magic = std.mem.readInt(u32, content[pos..][0..4], .little);\n                if (magic == WAL_MAGIC) {\n                    // Framed format: [magic:u32][crc:u32][len:u32][json][newline]\n                    const stored_crc = std.mem.readInt(u32, content[pos + 4 ..][0..4], .little);\n                    const len = std.mem.readInt(u32, content[pos + 8 ..][0..4], .little);\n\n                    const payload_start = pos + FRAME_HEADER_SIZE;\n                    const payload_end = payload_start + len;\n\n                    // Check for truncation\n                    if (payload_end > content.len) {\n                        // Truncated entry - skip to end (partial write from crash)\n                        break;\n                    }\n\n                    const json_payload = content[payload_start..payload_end];\n\n                    // Verify CRC32\n                    const computed_crc = std.hash.Crc32.hash(json_payload);\n                    if (computed_crc != stored_crc) {\n                        // CRC mismatch - corrupted entry, skip it\n                        // Try to find next entry by looking for next magic or newline\n                        pos = payload_end;\n                        if (pos < content.len and content[pos] == '\\n') {\n                            pos += 1;\n                        }\n                        continue;\n                    }\n\n                    // Parse the JSON payload\n                    if (self.parseEntry(json_payload)) |entry| {\n                        try entries.append(self.allocator, entry);\n                    } else |_| {\n                        // JSON parse error - skip\n                    }\n\n                    // Move past the entry (json + newline)\n                    pos = payload_end;\n                    if (pos < content.len and content[pos] == '\\n') {\n                        pos += 1;\n                    }\n                    continue;\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Fall back to legacy plain JSON line format\n            // Find the next newline\n            var line_end = pos;\n            while (line_end < content.len and content[line_end] != '\\n') {\n                line_end += 1;\n            }\n\n            if (line_end > pos) {\n                const line = content[pos..line_end];\n                if (self.parseEntry(line)) |entry| {\n                    try entries.append(self.allocator, entry);\n                } else |_| {\n                    // Skip malformed entries (graceful degradation)\n                }\n            }\n\n            pos = line_end;\n            if (pos < content.len and content[pos] == '\\n') {\n                pos += 1;\n            }\n        }\n\n        return entries.toOwnedSlice(self.allocator);\n    }\n\n    /// Parse a single WAL entry line.\n    fn parseEntry(self: *Self, line: []const u8) !ParsedWalEntry {\n        const parsed = std.json.parseFromSlice(\n            struct {\n                op: []const u8,\n                ts: i64,\n                seq: u64 = 0, // Default to 0 for legacy entries without seq\n                id: []const u8,\n                data: ?Issue,\n            },\n            self.allocator,\n            line,\n            .{ .ignore_unknown_fields = true, .allocate = .alloc_always },\n        ) catch return WalError.ParseError;\n        defer parsed.deinit();\n\n        const op = WalOp.fromString(parsed.value.op) orelse return WalError.InvalidOperation;\n\n        // Clone strings since parsed will be freed\n        const id = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, parsed.value.id);\n        errdefer self.allocator.free(id);\n\n        var data: ?Issue = null;\n        if (parsed.value.data) |issue| {\n            data = try issue.clone(self.allocator);\n        }\n\n        return ParsedWalEntry{\n            .op = op,\n            .ts = parsed.value.ts,\n            .seq = parsed.value.seq,\n            .id = id,\n            .data = data,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Replay WAL entries onto an IssueStore.\n    /// Applies operations in timestamp/sequence order.\n    /// Returns statistics about the replay including any failures.\n    pub fn replay(self: *Self, store: *IssueStore) !ReplayStats {\n        const entries = try self.readEntries();\n        defer {\n            for (entries) |*e| {\n                var entry = e.*;\n                entry.deinit(self.allocator);\n            }\n            self.allocator.free(entries);\n        }\n\n        // Sort by timestamp, then by sequence number for deterministic ordering\n        // when multiple entries have the same timestamp\n        std.mem.sortUnstable(ParsedWalEntry, @constCast(entries), {}, struct {\n            fn lessThan(_: void, a: ParsedWalEntry, b: ParsedWalEntry) bool {\n                if (a.ts != b.ts) return a.ts < b.ts;\n                return a.seq < b.seq;\n            }\n        }.lessThan);\n\n        // Track replay results\n        var stats = ReplayStats{};\n        var failure_ids: std.ArrayListUnmanaged([]const u8) = .{};\n        errdefer {\n            for (failure_ids.items) |id| {\n                self.allocator.free(id);\n            }\n            failure_ids.deinit(self.allocator);\n        }\n\n        // Apply each operation\n        for (entries) |entry| {\n            const result = self.applyEntry(store, entry);\n            switch (result) {\n                .applied => stats.applied += 1,\n                .skipped => stats.skipped += 1,\n                .failed => {\n                    stats.failed += 1;\n                    const id_copy = self.allocator.dupe(u8, entry.id) catch continue;\n                    failure_ids.append(self.allocator, id_copy) catch {\n                        self.allocator.free(id_copy);\n                    };\n                },\n            }\n        }\n\n        stats.failure_ids = failure_ids.toOwnedSlice(self.allocator) catch &.{};\n        return stats;\n    }\n\n    /// Result of applying a single WAL entry.\n    const ApplyResult = enum {\n        applied,\n        skipped,\n        failed,\n    };\n\n    /// Apply a single WAL entry to the store.\n    /// Returns the result of the operation.\n    fn applyEntry(self: *Self, store: *IssueStore, entry: ParsedWalEntry) ApplyResult {\n        _ = self;\n        switch (entry.op) {\n            .add => {\n                if (entry.data) |issue| {\n                    // Only insert if not already present\n                    if (!store.id_index.contains(issue.id)) {\n                        store.insert(issue) catch |err| switch (err) {\n                            error.DuplicateId => return .skipped, // Already exists\n                            else => return .failed,\n                        };\n                        return .applied;\n                    }\n                    return .skipped; // Already exists\n                }\n                return .skipped; // No data for add op\n            },\n            .update => {\n                if (entry.data) |issue| {\n                    // Update or insert\n                    if (store.id_index.contains(issue.id)) {\n                        // Full replacement for simplicity\n                        const idx = store.id_index.get(issue.id).?;\n                        var old = &store.issues.items[idx];\n                        old.deinit(store.allocator);\n                        store.issues.items[idx] = issue.clone(store.allocator) catch return .failed;\n                        return .applied;\n                    } else {\n                        store.insert(issue) catch return .failed;\n                        return .applied;\n                    }\n                }\n                return .skipped; // No data for update op\n            },\n            .close => {\n                store.update(entry.id, .{\n                    .status = .closed,\n                    .closed_at = std.time.timestamp(),\n                }, entry.ts) catch |err| switch (err) {\n                    error.IssueNotFound => return .skipped,\n                    else => return .failed,\n                };\n                return .applied;\n            },\n            .reopen => {\n                store.update(entry.id, .{\n                    .status = .open,\n                }, entry.ts) catch |err| switch (err) {\n                    error.IssueNotFound => return .skipped,\n                    else => return .failed,\n                };\n                return .applied;\n            },\n            .delete => {\n                store.delete(entry.id, entry.ts) catch |err| switch (err) {\n                    error.IssueNotFound => return .skipped,\n                    else => return .failed,\n                };\n                return .applied;\n            },\n            .set_blocked => {\n                store.update(entry.id, .{ .status = .blocked }, entry.ts) catch |err| switch (err) {\n                    error.IssueNotFound => return .skipped,\n                    else => return .failed,\n                };\n                return .applied;\n            },\n            .unset_blocked => {\n                store.update(entry.id, .{ .status = .open }, entry.ts) catch |err| switch (err) {\n                    error.IssueNotFound => return .skipped,\n                    else => return .failed,\n                };\n                return .applied;\n            },\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Get the number of entries in the WAL.\n    pub fn entryCount(self: *Self) !usize {\n        const entries = try self.readEntries();\n        defer {\n            for (entries) |*e| {\n                e.deinit(self.allocator);\n            }\n            self.allocator.free(entries);\n        }\n        return entries.len;\n    }\n\n    /// Get the size of the WAL file in bytes.\n    pub fn fileSize(self: *Self) !u64 {\n        const file = fs.cwd().openFile(self.wal_path, .{}) catch |err| switch (err) {\n            error.FileNotFound => return 0,\n            else => return err,\n        };\n        defer file.close();\n\n        const stat = try file.stat();\n        return stat.size;\n    }\n\n    /// Truncate the WAL file (used after compaction).\n    pub fn truncate(self: *Self) !void {\n        const dir = fs.cwd();\n        dir.deleteFile(self.wal_path) catch |err| switch (err) {\n            error.FileNotFound => {}, // Already empty\n            else => return err,\n        };\n    }\n\n    // Convenience methods for common operations\n\n    /// Add a new issue to the WAL.\n    pub fn addIssue(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n        try self.appendEntry(.{\n            .op = .add,\n            .ts = std.time.timestamp(),\n            .id = issue.id,\n            .data = issue,\n        });\n    }\n\n    /// Close an issue in the WAL.\n    pub fn closeIssue(self: *Self, id: []const u8) !void {\n        try self.appendEntry(.{\n            .op = .close,\n            .ts = std.time.timestamp(),\n            .id = id,\n            .data = null,\n        });\n    }\n\n    /// Reopen an issue in the WAL.\n    pub fn reopenIssue(self: *Self, id: []const u8) !void {\n        try self.appendEntry(.{\n            .op = .reopen,\n            .ts = std.time.timestamp(),\n            .id = id,\n            .data = null,\n        });\n    }\n\n    /// Update an issue in the WAL.\n    pub fn updateIssue(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n        try self.appendEntry(.{\n            .op = .update,\n            .ts = std.time.timestamp(),\n            .id = issue.id,\n            .data = issue,\n        });\n    }\n\n    /// Delete an issue in the WAL (tombstone).\n    pub fn deleteIssue(self: *Self, id: []const u8) !void {\n        try self.appendEntry(.{\n            .op = .delete,\n            .ts = std.time.timestamp(),\n            .id = id,\n            .data = null,\n        });\n    }\n\n    /// Set an issue as blocked in the WAL.\n    pub fn setBlocked(self: *Self, id: []const u8) !void {\n        try self.appendEntry(.{\n            .op = .set_blocked,\n            .ts = std.time.timestamp(),\n            .id = id,\n            .data = null,\n        });\n    }\n\n    /// Unset blocked status in the WAL.\n    pub fn unsetBlocked(self: *Self, id: []const u8) !void {\n        try self.appendEntry(.{\n            .op = .unset_blocked,\n            .ts = std.time.timestamp(),\n            .id = id,\n            .data = null,\n        });\n    }\n};\n\n// --- Tests ---\n\ntest \"WalOp.toString and fromString roundtrip\" {\n    const ops = [_]WalOp{ .add, .update, .close, .reopen, .delete, .set_blocked, .unset_blocked };\n    for (ops) |op| {\n        const str = op.toString();\n        const parsed = WalOp.fromString(str);\n        try std.testing.expect(parsed != null);\n        try std.testing.expectEqual(op, parsed.?);\n    }\n}\n\ntest \"WalOp.fromString returns null for unknown\" {\n    try std.testing.expect(WalOp.fromString(\"unknown\") == null);\n    try std.testing.expect(WalOp.fromString(\"\") == null);\n}\n\ntest \"Wal.init and deinit\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"wal_init\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    var wal = try Wal.init(test_dir, allocator);\n    defer wal.deinit();\n\n    // Generation-aware path (generation 1 by default)\n    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.endsWith(u8, wal.wal_path, \"/beads.wal.1\"));\n    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.endsWith(u8, wal.lock_path, \"/beads.lock\"));\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u64, 1), wal.generation);\n}\n\ntest \"Wal.rotateGeneration creates new generation\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"wal_rotate\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    var wal = try Wal.init(test_dir, allocator);\n    defer wal.deinit();\n\n    // Initial generation is 1\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u64, 1), wal.getGeneration());\n\n    // rotateGeneration must be called with lock held (simulates compactor behavior)\n    // Acquire lock before rotating\n    var lock = BeadsLock.acquire(wal.lock_path) catch unreachable;\n\n    // Rotate to new generation\n    const new_gen = try wal.rotateGeneration();\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u64, 2), new_gen);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u64, 2), wal.getGeneration());\n    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.endsWith(u8, wal.wal_path, \"/beads.wal.2\"));\n\n    // Rotate again\n    const newer_gen = try wal.rotateGeneration();\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u64, 3), newer_gen);\n    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.endsWith(u8, wal.wal_path, \"/beads.wal.3\"));\n\n    lock.release();\n}\n\ntest \"Wal.refreshGeneration detects external changes\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"wal_refresh\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    var wal = try Wal.init(test_dir, allocator);\n    defer wal.deinit();\n\n    // Initially generation 1\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u64, 1), wal.getGeneration());\n\n    // Externally update generation (simulates another process doing compaction)\n    var gen = Generation.init(test_dir, allocator);\n    try gen.write(5);\n\n    // Refresh should detect the change\n    const changed = try wal.refreshGeneration();\n    try std.testing.expect(changed);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u64, 5), wal.getGeneration());\n    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.endsWith(u8, wal.wal_path, \"/beads.wal.5\"));\n}\n\ntest \"Wal.readEntries returns empty for missing file\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"wal_missing\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    var wal = try Wal.init(test_dir, allocator);\n    defer wal.deinit();\n\n    const entries = try wal.readEntries();\n    defer allocator.free(entries);\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), entries.len);\n}\n\ntest \"Wal.appendEntry and readEntries roundtrip\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"wal_roundtrip\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    var wal = try Wal.init(test_dir, allocator);\n    defer wal.deinit();\n\n    const issue = Issue.init(\"bd-test1\", \"Test Issue\", 1706540000);\n\n    try wal.appendEntry(.{\n        .op = .add,\n        .ts = 1706540000,\n        .id = \"bd-test1\",\n        .data = issue,\n    });\n\n    try wal.appendEntry(.{\n        .op = .close,\n        .ts = 1706540001,\n        .id = \"bd-test1\",\n        .data = null,\n    });\n\n    const entries = try wal.readEntries();\n    defer {\n        for (entries) |*e| {\n            var entry = e.*;\n            entry.deinit(allocator);\n        }\n        allocator.free(entries);\n    }\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 2), entries.len);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(WalOp.add, entries[0].op);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(WalOp.close, entries[1].op);\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"bd-test1\", entries[0].id);\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"bd-test1\", entries[1].id);\n    try std.testing.expect(entries[0].data != null);\n    try std.testing.expect(entries[1].data == null);\n}\n\ntest \"Wal.replay applies operations to store\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"wal_replay\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    // Create WAL with operations\n    var wal = try Wal.init(test_dir, allocator);\n    defer wal.deinit();\n\n    const issue = Issue.init(\"bd-replay1\", \"Replay Test\", 1706540000);\n\n    try wal.appendEntry(.{\n        .op = .add,\n        .ts = 1706540000,\n        .id = \"bd-replay1\",\n        .data = issue,\n    });\n\n    // Create store and replay\n    const jsonl_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ test_dir, \"issues.jsonl\" });\n    defer allocator.free(jsonl_path);\n\n    var store = IssueStore.init(allocator, jsonl_path);\n    defer store.deinit();\n\n    var stats = try wal.replay(&store);\n    defer stats.deinit(allocator);\n\n    // Verify replay succeeded\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 1), stats.applied);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), stats.failed);\n\n    // Verify issue was added\n    try std.testing.expect(try store.exists(\"bd-replay1\"));\n    const retrieved = try store.get(\"bd-replay1\");\n    try std.testing.expect(retrieved != null);\n    var r = retrieved.?;\n    defer r.deinit(allocator);\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"Replay Test\", r.title);\n}\n\ntest \"Wal.entryCount\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"wal_count\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    var wal = try Wal.init(test_dir, allocator);\n    defer wal.deinit();\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), try wal.entryCount());\n\n    const issue = Issue.init(\"bd-count1\", \"Count Test\", 1706540000);\n    try wal.appendEntry(.{ .op = .add, .ts = 1706540000, .id = \"bd-count1\", .data = issue });\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 1), try wal.entryCount());\n\n    try wal.appendEntry(.{ .op = .close, .ts = 1706540001, .id = \"bd-count1\", .data = null });\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 2), try wal.entryCount());\n}\n\ntest \"Wal.truncate clears WAL\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try {"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_012gbobdvS5z5k7V7JH5Dhzk","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→//! WAL Compaction for beads_zig.\n     2→//!\n     3→//! Merges WAL entries into the main JSONL file when the WAL exceeds thresholds.\n     4→//! This consolidates state and keeps the WAL small for fast reads.\n     5→//!\n     6→//! Compaction flow (with generation-based safety):\n     7→//! 1. Acquire BeadsLock (exclusive)\n     8→//! 2. Load beads.jsonl into memory\n     9→//! 3. Replay current generation's WAL operations\n    10→//! 4. Write merged state to beads.jsonl.tmp\n    11→//! 5. fsync for durability\n    12→//! 6. Atomic rename over beads.jsonl\n    13→//! 7. Rotate to new generation (increment beads.generation, new beads.wal.N)\n    14→//! 8. Clean up old generation WAL files\n    15→//! 9. Release lock\n    16→//!\n    17→//! Generation-based rotation prevents reader/compactor races:\n    18→//! - Old WAL file remains readable during compaction\n    19→//! - New generation number signals readers to refresh\n    20→//! - Readers retry if generation changed during read\n    21→\n    22→const std = @import(\"std\");\n    23→const fs = std.fs;\n    24→const BeadsLock = @import(\"lock.zig\").BeadsLock;\n    25→const Wal = @import(\"wal.zig\").Wal;\n    26→const JsonlFile = @import(\"jsonl.zig\").JsonlFile;\n    27→const IssueStore = @import(\"store.zig\").IssueStore;\n    28→const Generation = @import(\"generation.zig\").Generation;\n    29→const test_util = @import(\"../test_util.zig\");\n    30→\n    31→pub const CompactError = error{\n    32→    LockFailed,\n    33→    CompactionFailed,\n    34→    WriteError,\n    35→    AtomicRenameFailed,\n    36→    OutOfMemory,\n    37→};\n    38→\n    39→/// Thresholds for automatic compaction.\n    40→pub const CompactionThresholds = struct {\n    41→    /// Maximum number of WAL entries before compaction.\n    42→    max_entries: usize = 100,\n    43→    /// Maximum WAL file size in bytes before compaction.\n    44→    max_bytes: u64 = 100 * 1024, // 100KB\n    45→};\n    46→\n    47→/// Statistics about the WAL for monitoring.\n    48→pub const WalStats = struct {\n    49→    entry_count: usize,\n    50→    file_size: u64,\n    51→    needs_compaction: bool,\n    52→};\n    53→\n    54→/// Compactor handles WAL compaction operations.\n    55→pub const Compactor = struct {\n    56→    beads_dir: []const u8,\n    57→    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    58→    thresholds: CompactionThresholds,\n    59→\n    60→    const Self = @This();\n    61→\n    62→    pub fn init(beads_dir: []const u8, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) Self {\n    63→        return .{\n    64→            .beads_dir = beads_dir,\n    65→            .allocator = allocator,\n    66→            .thresholds = .{},\n    67→        };\n    68→    }\n    69→\n    70→    pub fn initWithThresholds(beads_dir: []const u8, allocator: std.mem.Allocator, thresholds: CompactionThresholds) Self {\n    71→        return .{\n    72→            .beads_dir = beads_dir,\n    73→            .allocator = allocator,\n    74→            .thresholds = thresholds,\n    75→        };\n    76→    }\n    77→\n    78→    /// Get current WAL statistics.\n    79→    pub fn walStats(self: *Self) !WalStats {\n    80→        var wal = try Wal.init(self.beads_dir, self.allocator);\n    81→        defer wal.deinit();\n    82→\n    83→        const entry_count = try wal.entryCount();\n    84→        const file_size = try wal.fileSize();\n    85→\n    86→        return .{\n    87→            .entry_count = entry_count,\n    88→            .file_size = file_size,\n    89→            .needs_compaction = entry_count >= self.thresholds.max_entries or\n    90→                file_size >= self.thresholds.max_bytes,\n    91→        };\n    92→    }\n    93→\n    94→    /// Trigger compaction if WAL exceeds threshold.\n    95→    /// Returns true if compaction was performed.\n    96→    pub fn maybeCompact(self: *Self) !bool {\n    97→        const stats = try self.walStats();\n    98→        if (stats.needs_compaction) {\n    99→            try self.compact();\n   100→            return true;\n   101→        }\n   102→        return false;\n   103→    }\n   104→\n   105→    /// Compact WAL into main file with generation-based safety.\n   106→    /// 1. Acquire BeadsLock (exclusive)\n   107→    /// 2. Load beads.jsonl into memory\n   108→    /// 3. Replay current generation's WAL operations\n   109→    /// 4. Write merged state to beads.jsonl.tmp\n   110→    /// 5. fsync for durability\n   111→    /// 6. Atomic rename over beads.jsonl\n   112→    /// 7. Rotate to new generation (creates new WAL file)\n   113→    /// 8. Clean up old WAL files\n   114→    /// 9. Release lock\n   115→    pub fn compact(self: *Self) !void {\n   116→        const lock_path = try std.fs.path.join(self.allocator, &.{ self.beads_dir, \"beads.lock\" });\n   117→        defer self.allocator.free(lock_path);\n   118→\n   119→        const jsonl_path = try std.fs.path.join(self.allocator, &.{ self.beads_dir, \"beads.jsonl\" });\n   120→        defer self.allocator.free(jsonl_path);\n   121→\n   122→        // 1. Acquire exclusive lock\n   123→        var lock = BeadsLock.acquire(lock_path) catch return CompactError.LockFailed;\n   124→        defer lock.release();\n   125→\n   126→        // 2. Load main file into memory\n   127→        var store = IssueStore.init(self.allocator, jsonl_path);\n   128→        defer store.deinit();\n   129→\n   130→        store.loadFromFile() catch |err| switch (err) {\n   131→            error.FileNotFound => {}, // Empty main file is OK\n   132→            else => return CompactError.CompactionFailed,\n   133→        };\n   134→\n   135→        // 3. Replay WAL operations (using current generation)\n   136→        var wal = try Wal.init(self.beads_dir, self.allocator);\n   137→        defer wal.deinit();\n   138→\n   139→        const old_generation = wal.getGeneration();\n   140→\n   141→        var replay_stats = wal.replay(&store) catch return CompactError.CompactionFailed;\n   142→        defer replay_stats.deinit(self.allocator);\n   143→        // Note: During compaction we proceed even if some replays failed,\n   144→        // since the remaining operations should still be compacted.\n   145→\n   146→        // 4-6. Write merged state atomically\n   147→        try self.writeAtomically(jsonl_path, store.issues.items);\n   148→\n   149→        // 7. Rotate to new generation (creates fresh WAL file, cleans up old ones)\n   150→        // This is the key change: instead of truncating the old WAL (which races\n   151→        // with readers), we rotate to a new generation. Readers will detect the\n   152→        // generation change and retry with the new WAL file.\n   153→        _ = wal.rotateGeneration() catch {\n   154→            // If rotation fails, fall back to traditional truncation\n   155→            // This maintains backwards compatibility but loses race safety\n   156→            wal.truncate() catch return CompactError.CompactionFailed;\n   157→            return;\n   158→        };\n   159→\n   160→        // 8. Delete old generation's WAL file (safe now since generation incremented)\n   161→        // Readers that were mid-read will retry with new generation\n   162→        self.deleteOldWal(old_generation);\n   163→    }\n   164→\n   165→    /// Delete old generation's WAL file.\n   166→    fn deleteOldWal(self: *Self, old_gen: u64) void {\n   167→        var gen = Generation.init(self.beads_dir, self.allocator);\n   168→        const old_wal_path = gen.walPath(old_gen) catch return;\n   169→        defer self.allocator.free(old_wal_path);\n   170→\n   171→        fs.cwd().deleteFile(old_wal_path) catch {};\n   172→    }\n   173→\n   174→    /// Write issues to file atomically (temp file + fsync + rename).\n   175→    fn writeAtomically(self: *Self, target_path: []const u8, issues: []const @import(\"../models/issue.zig\").Issue) !void {\n   176→        const dir = fs.cwd();\n   177→\n   178→        // Create temp file path\n   179→        var tmp_path_buf: [std.fs.max_path_bytes]u8 = undefined;\n   180→        const tmp_path = std.fmt.bufPrint(&tmp_path_buf, \"{s}.tmp.{d}\", .{\n   181→            target_path,\n   182→            std.time.milliTimestamp(),\n   183→        }) catch return CompactError.WriteError;\n   184→\n   185→        // Write to temp file\n   186→        const tmp_file = dir.createFile(tmp_path, .{}) catch return CompactError.WriteError;\n   187→        errdefer {\n   188→            tmp_file.close();\n   189→            dir.deleteFile(tmp_path) catch {};\n   190→        }\n   191→\n   192→        // Serialize and write each issue\n   193→        for (issues) |issue| {\n   194→            const json_bytes = std.json.Stringify.valueAlloc(self.allocator, issue, .{}) catch return CompactError.WriteError;\n   195→            defer self.allocator.free(json_bytes);\n   196→\n   197→            tmp_file.writeAll(json_bytes) catch return CompactError.WriteError;\n   198→            tmp_file.writeAll(\"\\n\") catch return CompactError.WriteError;\n   199→        }\n   200→\n   201→        // 5. fsync for durability\n   202→        tmp_file.sync() catch return CompactError.WriteError;\n   203→        tmp_file.close();\n   204→\n   205→        // 6. Atomic rename\n   206→        dir.rename(tmp_path, target_path) catch return CompactError.AtomicRenameFailed;\n   207→    }\n   208→\n   209→    /// Force compaction regardless of thresholds.\n   210→    /// Use this for explicit sync operations.\n   211→    pub fn forceCompact(self: *Self) !void {\n   212→        try self.compact();\n   213→    }\n   214→};\n   215→\n   216→// --- Tests ---\n You can still analyze existing code, write reports, or answer questions about the code behavior.\n</system-reminder>\n"}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"db18cbd5-5684-4054-8b1d-9d87e9580670","uuid":"41e1e599-041f-4a47-b971-1f2e57f1e171","tool_use_result":{"type":"text","file":{"filePath":"/home/hotschmoe/beads_zig/src/storage/compact.zig","content":"//! WAL Compaction for beads_zig.\n//!\n//! Merges WAL entries into the main JSONL file when the WAL exceeds thresholds.\n//! This consolidates state and keeps the WAL small for fast reads.\n//!\n//! Compaction flow (with generation-based safety):\n//! 1. Acquire BeadsLock (exclusive)\n//! 2. Load beads.jsonl into memory\n//! 3. Replay current generation's WAL operations\n//! 4. Write merged state to beads.jsonl.tmp\n//! 5. fsync for durability\n//! 6. Atomic rename over beads.jsonl\n//! 7. Rotate to new generation (increment beads.generation, new beads.wal.N)\n//! 8. Clean up old generation WAL files\n//! 9. Release lock\n//!\n//! Generation-based rotation prevents reader/compactor races:\n//! - Old WAL file remains readable during compaction\n//! - New generation number signals readers to refresh\n//! - Readers retry if generation changed during read\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\nconst fs = std.fs;\nconst BeadsLock = @import(\"lock.zig\").BeadsLock;\nconst Wal = @import(\"wal.zig\").Wal;\nconst JsonlFile = @import(\"jsonl.zig\").JsonlFile;\nconst IssueStore = @import(\"store.zig\").IssueStore;\nconst Generation = @import(\"generation.zig\").Generation;\nconst test_util = @import(\"../test_util.zig\");\n\npub const CompactError = error{\n    LockFailed,\n    CompactionFailed,\n    WriteError,\n    AtomicRenameFailed,\n    OutOfMemory,\n};\n\n/// Thresholds for automatic compaction.\npub const CompactionThresholds = struct {\n    /// Maximum number of WAL entries before compaction.\n    max_entries: usize = 100,\n    /// Maximum WAL file size in bytes before compaction.\n    max_bytes: u64 = 100 * 1024, // 100KB\n};\n\n/// Statistics about the WAL for monitoring.\npub const WalStats = struct {\n    entry_count: usize,\n    file_size: u64,\n    needs_compaction: bool,\n};\n\n/// Compactor handles WAL compaction operations.\npub const Compactor = struct {\n    beads_dir: []const u8,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    thresholds: CompactionThresholds,\n\n    const Self = @This();\n\n    pub fn init(beads_dir: []const u8, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) Self {\n        return .{\n            .beads_dir = beads_dir,\n            .allocator = allocator,\n            .thresholds = .{},\n        };\n    }\n\n    pub fn initWithThresholds(beads_dir: []const u8, allocator: std.mem.Allocator, thresholds: CompactionThresholds) Self {\n        return .{\n            .beads_dir = beads_dir,\n            .allocator = allocator,\n            .thresholds = thresholds,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Get current WAL statistics.\n    pub fn walStats(self: *Self) !WalStats {\n        var wal = try Wal.init(self.beads_dir, self.allocator);\n        defer wal.deinit();\n\n        const entry_count = try wal.entryCount();\n        const file_size = try wal.fileSize();\n\n        return .{\n            .entry_count = entry_count,\n            .file_size = file_size,\n            .needs_compaction = entry_count >= self.thresholds.max_entries or\n                file_size >= self.thresholds.max_bytes,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Trigger compaction if WAL exceeds threshold.\n    /// Returns true if compaction was performed.\n    pub fn maybeCompact(self: *Self) !bool {\n        const stats = try self.walStats();\n        if (stats.needs_compaction) {\n            try self.compact();\n            return true;\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /// Compact WAL into main file with generation-based safety.\n    /// 1. Acquire BeadsLock (exclusive)\n    /// 2. Load beads.jsonl into memory\n    /// 3. Replay current generation's WAL operations\n    /// 4. Write merged state to beads.jsonl.tmp\n    /// 5. fsync for durability\n    /// 6. Atomic rename over beads.jsonl\n    /// 7. Rotate to new generation (creates new WAL file)\n    /// 8. Clean up old WAL files\n    /// 9. Release lock\n    pub fn compact(self: *Self) !void {\n        const lock_path = try std.fs.path.join(self.allocator, &.{ self.beads_dir, \"beads.lock\" });\n        defer self.allocator.free(lock_path);\n\n        const jsonl_path = try std.fs.path.join(self.allocator, &.{ self.beads_dir, \"beads.jsonl\" });\n        defer self.allocator.free(jsonl_path);\n\n        // 1. Acquire exclusive lock\n        var lock = BeadsLock.acquire(lock_path) catch return CompactError.LockFailed;\n        defer lock.release();\n\n        // 2. Load main file into memory\n        var store = IssueStore.init(self.allocator, jsonl_path);\n        defer store.deinit();\n\n        store.loadFromFile() catch |err| switch (err) {\n            error.FileNotFound => {}, // Empty main file is OK\n            else => return CompactError.CompactionFailed,\n        };\n\n        // 3. Replay WAL operations (using current generation)\n        var wal = try Wal.init(self.beads_dir, self.allocator);\n        defer wal.deinit();\n\n        const old_generation = wal.getGeneration();\n\n        var replay_stats = wal.replay(&store) catch return CompactError.CompactionFailed;\n        defer replay_stats.deinit(self.allocator);\n        // Note: During compaction we proceed even if some replays failed,\n        // since the remaining operations should still be compacted.\n\n        // 4-6. Write merged state atomically\n        try self.writeAtomically(jsonl_path, store.issues.items);\n\n        // 7. Rotate to new generation (creates fresh WAL file, cleans up old ones)\n        // This is the key change: instead of truncating the old WAL (which races\n        // with readers), we rotate to a new generation. Readers will detect the\n        // generation change and retry with the new WAL file.\n        _ = wal.rotateGeneration() catch {\n            // If rotation fails, fall back to traditional truncation\n            // This maintains backwards compatibility but loses race safety\n            wal.truncate() catch return CompactError.CompactionFailed;\n            return;\n        };\n\n        // 8. Delete old generation's WAL file (safe now since generation incremented)\n        // Readers that were mid-read will retry with new generation\n        self.deleteOldWal(old_generation);\n    }\n\n    /// Delete old generation's WAL file.\n    fn deleteOldWal(self: *Self, old_gen: u64) void {\n        var gen = Generation.init(self.beads_dir, self.allocator);\n        const old_wal_path = gen.walPath(old_gen) catch return;\n        defer self.allocator.free(old_wal_path);\n\n        fs.cwd().deleteFile(old_wal_path) catch {};\n    }\n\n    /// Write issues to file atomically (temp file + fsync + rename).\n    fn writeAtomically(self: *Self, target_path: []const u8, issues: []const @import(\"../models/issue.zig\").Issue) !void {\n        const dir = fs.cwd();\n\n        // Create temp file path\n        var tmp_path_buf: [std.fs.max_path_bytes]u8 = undefined;\n        const tmp_path = std.fmt.bufPrint(&tmp_path_buf, \"{s}.tmp.{d}\", .{\n            target_path,\n            std.time.milliTimestamp(),\n        }) catch return CompactError.WriteError;\n\n        // Write to temp file\n        const tmp_file = dir.createFile(tmp_path, .{}) catch return CompactError.WriteError;\n        errdefer {\n            tmp_file.close();\n            dir.deleteFile(tmp_path) catch {};\n        }\n\n        // Serialize and write each issue\n        for (issues) |issue| {\n            const json_bytes = std.json.Stringify.valueAlloc(self.allocator, issue, .{}) catch return CompactError.WriteError;\n            defer self.allocator.free(json_bytes);\n\n            tmp_file.writeAll(json_bytes) catch return CompactError.WriteError;\n            tmp_file.writeAll(\"\\n\") catch return CompactError.WriteError;\n        }\n\n        // 5. fsync for durability\n        tmp_file.sync() catch return CompactError.WriteError;\n        tmp_file.close();\n\n        // 6. Atomic rename\n        dir.rename(tmp_path, target_path) catch return CompactError.AtomicRenameFailed;\n    }\n\n    /// Force compaction regardless of thresholds.\n    /// Use this for explicit sync operations.\n    pub fn forceCompact(self: *Self) !void {\n        try self.compact();\n    }\n};\n\n// --- Tests ---\n\ntest \"Compactor.init\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n\n    const compactor = Compactor.init(\".beads\", allocator);\n\n    // Verify default thresholds\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 100), compactor.thresholds.max_entries);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u64, 100 * 1024), compactor.thresholds.max_bytes);\n}\n\ntest \"Compactor.initWithThresholds\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n\n    const compactor = Compactor.initWithThresholds(\".beads\", allocator, .{\n        .max_entries = 50,\n        .max_bytes = 50 * 1024,\n    });\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 50), compactor.thresholds.max_entries);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u64, 50 * 1024), compactor.thresholds.max_bytes);\n}\n\ntest \"Compactor.walStats returns stats for empty WAL\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"compact_stats_empty\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    var compactor = Compactor.init(test_dir, allocator);\n    const stats = try compactor.walStats();\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), stats.entry_count);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u64, 0), stats.file_size);\n    try std.testing.expect(!stats.needs_compaction);\n}\n\ntest \"Compactor.walStats detects when compaction needed\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"compact_stats_needed\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    // Create WAL with some entries\n    var wal = try Wal.init(test_dir, allocator);\n    defer wal.deinit();\n\n    const Issue = @import(\"../models/issue.zig\").Issue;\n    const issue = Issue.init(\"bd-test1\", \"Test Issue\", 1706540000);\n\n    // Add entries up to threshold\n    for (0..5) |i| {\n        try wal.appendEntry(.{\n            .op = .add,\n            .ts = 1706540000 + @as(i64, @intCast(i)),\n            .id = \"bd-test1\",\n            .data = issue,\n        });\n    }\n\n    // Test with
